    "date_format/date_range_with_short_weekday_short_month": function date_formatDate_range_with_short_weekday_short_month(args) {
      return selectItem(args, {
        "1": function _() {
          return getArg("short_weekday", args) + ", " + getArg("day_of_month", args) + " " + getArg("short_month_name", args) + " - " + getArg("short_weekday_until", args) + ", " + getArg("day_of_month_until", args) + " " + getArg("short_month_name_until", args);
        },
        "date_with_weekday_time_at": function date_with_weekday_time_at() {
          return "date_range_with_short_weekday_short_month";
        },
        "other": function other() {
          return "";
        }
      });
    },
    "date_format/date_with_short_weekday_with_year": function date_formatDate_with_short_weekday_with_year(args) {
      return selectItem(args, {
        "1": function _() {
          return getArg("short_weekday", args) + ", " + getArg("day_of_month", args) + " de " + getArg("month_name", args) + " de " + getArg("full_year", args);
        },
        "date_with_weekday_time_at": function date_with_weekday_time_at() {
          return "date_with_short_weekday_with_year";
        },
        "other": function other() {
          return "";
        }
      });
    },
    "date_format/date_with_short_weekday_without_year": function date_formatDate_with_short_weekday_without_year(args) {
      return selectItem(args, {
        "1": function _() {
          return getArg("short_weekday", args) + ", " + getArg("day_of_month", args) + " de " + getArg("month_name", args);
        },
        "date_with_weekday_time_at": function date_with_weekday_time_at() {
          return "date_with_short_weekday_without_year";
        },
        "other": function other() {
          return "";
        }
